Livelihood Self-Help Society Proceeds with Opening Mobile Stores 91

Another Way Out for Refugees

After the September 18th Incident, North Shanghai suffered severely from the Japanese army's ravages, and countless compatriots were displaced. There are still more than 40,000 people with skills who cannot be settled. Although various relief societies have tried their best to accommodate them, the cost is huge and difficult to support for a long time. Recently, a Livelihood Self-Help Society was organized, which plans to cooperate with the refugee factories of the Livelihood Improvement Society to implement the opening of mobile stores. The store clerks are filled by refugees, specializing in selling domestic goods and making their own profits. The plan is very precise. The society's preparatory committee has now been established, and the promoters are Li Denghui, Hu Shuhua, Li Zhaohuan, Liang Shichun, Ji Kangfu, Wang Gang, Song Fuhua, and Ye Jingfeng. The steps are to first contact various shelters and simultaneously raise start-up funds from charitable organizations and philanthropists. It is said that the method is to form a group of five people, and each group needs about 100 yuan for start-up costs. The first batch plans to form 100 groups, select refugees with sales experience, and then add new training before starting.

Chauffeur Sacrifices Himself for His Master Ma Changsheng's Son Kidnapped 93

Ma Yifa, Fifteen Years Old

Wearing Diamond Ring Worth Over a Thousand Gold

Kidnappers in Desperation Kill Chauffeur

Hostage Once Kidnapped Before

Ma Yifa, the fifth son of Ma Changsheng, a well-known antique merchant in this city, was kidnapped in front of his residence on Glock Road in the French Concession at around 7:00 a.m. yesterday. Xia Baosheng, the chauffeur of the Ma residence, was shot dead by the bandits on the spot because he bravely resisted. The detailed information is recorded as follows:

Antique Market Ma Changsheng, a native of Jinling, is 57 years old and follows Islam. He started his business by operating antiques, jade, and jewelry and owns a huge amount of capital. He built a large building at the corner of Glock Road and Ailai Ge Road in the French Concession, with the address numbers 74 to 76, with the Ma Chang Ji brand hanging at the door. On the surface, it is a residence and a business, but it is actually a large-scale antique market. Ma's trade is mostly with foreign businessmen, especially with the Three Islands, so he is well-known. Almost all antique dealers at home and abroad know Ma Chang Ji.

Yifa Limps Ma has many children. His elder and younger brothers are all adults. The fifth son is named Yifa, is 15 years old, and has a limp. The sixth son, Shunfa, is 12 years old, and another son is named Yongfu, is 13 years old. These three sons are studying at Gezhi Public School on Beihai Road in the Public Concession. They use their own car No. 262 to travel back and forth every morning and evening. Xia Baosheng (56 years old) and Xia Shunde (23 years old), father and son, are hired as chauffeurs. Xia lives at 433 Bopai Road, Datiebang. He goes early and returns late every day and serves diligently, which is deeply trusted by the master.

Bandits Suddenly Arrive At 7:30 a.m. yesterday morning, the chauffeur Xia Baosheng drove the car as usual, intending to send the young masters to school. At that time, he parked the car outside the back door. Yifa and the other three walked into the car in a row. As soon as they were seated, Xia Baosheng was about to start the engine when four bandits with a Northern accent suddenly rushed out of the alleys of Fuqingli and Guianli across the road, two holding box cannons and two holding pistols. Two bandits first guarded the left and right doors of the car, and the other two bandits ran to the chauffeur.

Chauffeur Sacrifices Master At this critical moment, the chauffeur Xia Baosheng saw that the situation was not good and knew that he had encountered bandits. He quickly locked the hidden lock installed on the car door with his backhand, and shouted for help loudly. The bandits repeatedly pried the handle of the car door, but they could not push it even a little. The bandits were anxious and smashed the glass with the butt of the gun, intending to reach in and open the door. Xia resisted bravely, and the bandits became even more anxious and fired a shot at Xia. The bullet hit the right chest breast, penetrated the back, and died in the car.

Kidnapping the Hostage After the bandits killed the chauffeur, they hurriedly opened the car door, pulled Yifa out of the car, and put him in a bandit car parked near Ningbo Road. A bandit driver drove at full speed and escaped without a trace. At that time, Ma's family had already heard the police, and hurriedly reported to the Songshan Road Police Station by phone, frantically sounded the siren, and the male and female servants rushed out to take the two children, Shunfa and Yongfu, out of the car. However, the two children were young and timid. They witnessed the chauffeur being shot and the elder brother being kidnapped, and they were already as pale as wood and lifeless.

Diamond Ring Worth a Lot After a while, Chinese and Western detectives from the Songshan Road Police Station and the special agency rushed to the scene one after another and rounded up in all directions. However, the bandits had already fled far away without a trace. They asked the nearby shops about the bandits' clothes and appearance, and reported to the head of the police. A detective sent Xia Baoshan's body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch autopsy office to wait for the court to send a court inspector to inspect it today. It is said that Yifa is young and intelligent and is loved by his parents. When he was kidnapped, he was wearing a diamond ring worth 1,350 yuan on his finger. However, Yifa was kidnapped once eight years ago and lived in the bandit's den for two months. Later, he was rescued by the French police. After the incident, the police found that Zhang Zhihua, the bodyguard who had recently stopped working at Ma's house, was suspected and was summoned for questioning. He was ordered to be handed over to Bao Houhe. The police station notified the Public Concession Police Station and the Huajie Public Security Bureau to investigate the bandits' whereabouts. Therefore, the Public Concession inspected pedestrians and questioned cars very strictly last night.

Vengeance Killing of Ji Zhongtang 94

Tragic Case in the Japanese-Occupied Area

Head, Breast, Eyes, Waist, and Ribs All Hit by Bullets

Ji Zhongtang, 34 years old, a native of Yancheng, used to be a detective in the Fifth District of Zhabei. He was detained by the local court and sentenced to two years in prison for falsely accusing good people of theft, injuring suspects, and extorting silk machines, and was sent to prison for execution. He was released last month. The day before yesterday, Ji went to visit his apprentice Zhang Xiaowanzi, who lived in Zhangjiaxiang, Hujia Muqiao, and went to a small teahouse opened by Wei Cheshi to drink tea with Zhang. Unexpectedly, his enemies found out and gathered many people, each holding a pistol, and said to Ji, "The three-year revenge has finally been met. You have thrown yourself into the trap." Ji knew that it was difficult to escape, and wanted to beg for mercy, but the bullets had already come. Ji immediately dodged, but several shots were fired, and Ji suffered five or six gunshot wounds to the head, breast, eyes, waist, and ribs. He immediately fell to the ground and died in a pool of blood. The murderers all fled. According to Zhang Xiaowanzi, the murderers were the rogue Wang Shubao, Wang Sanmingzi, Zheng Xiaoheizi, etc. Afterwards, the Japanese military headquarters sent personnel to the scene to verify the situation, and the body was coffined. Yesterday, the local security guard Xu Jinlin, together with Zhang Xiaowanzi Wei Cheshi, carried the body coffin to the Nanshi to request the local court to inspect the body. Wu, the prosecutor, opened the coffin to inspect it, filled in the body form, and ordered it to be carried back to wait for the arrest of the murderer.

Fall in Love at First Sight in the Hospital and Live with a Widow 95

Love Fades Over Time and Sues in Court

Criminal Case Could Not Be Established

Diamond Ring and Cash Were Ordered to be Returned

Yang Xianbang Imprisoned Without Bail

Yang Xianbang, the former measuring director of the Industrial Patrol Donation Bureau, is now a consultant to the Henan Security Department. When he was working in the Industrial Patrol Donation Bureau, he went to the Robert Li Hospital on Manufacturing Bureau Road for treatment because of illness. There was a young widow, Tao Shuzhen, in the hospital, and he fell in love with her. From then on, they fell in love with each other, and like Sima Xiangru and Zhuo Wenjun, they hit it off. Therefore, they lived together next to the South Guild Hall. Since Yang's business was dismissed after the revolution, their love gradually cooled down and eventually broke down. Tao once hired a lawyer to sue Yang Xianbang for demolition, seduction, and fraud. As a result, he could not be punished criminally, and the civil court ruled that Yang Xianbang should return a diamond ring and 3,000 yuan in cash to Tao Shuzhen. The execution has been confirmed, and Yang immediately went to Henan to take office. However, the rent of the house where Tao lived was paid by Yang. After the love broke down, the rent was not paid. Luo Shushi, the accountant of the South Guild Hall, requested the local court to order the relocation, which has been approved. Tao believed that this was a trick of Yang's, so she sued Yang and his wife Wang Weilin for bigamy and abandonment, and also implicated Luo Shushi. The reason was that Yang and she had lived together and had a three-chapter covenant, and the relatives considered them husband and wife. The court repeatedly arrested Yang but failed to arrive and issued a warrant for arrest. He was arrested at the Oriental Hotel. Tao pointed out that Wang Yueying, a girlfriend in the same room, was his wife who committed bigamy. After being prosecuted by the prosecutor, the criminal court has repeatedly tried the case. The day before yesterday, the court ruled that the Tao Shuzhen's lawsuit against Yang Xianbang, Wang Weilin, and Wang Yueying was not accepted in part, and Luo Shushi was not guilty. Unexpectedly, the criminal court had just made a ruling, and the civil execution court had learned that Yang Xianbang had been arrested, and ordered the officer Wang Guocheng to bring Yang from the criminal court. After questioning, he ordered him to be bailed out to pay off the debt. At that time, there was no bail, so he was ordered to be detained. The river of love has many obstacles, which can be seen.

The Issue of Director Ye Shantao in the Riyue Bank Case 96

The Key Lies in Huang Chuqiu's Letter

Witness Gan Yuesong Failed to Appear Yesterday

After the collapse of Riyue Bank, its creditor, Dong Longxing, and others filed a lawsuit against Ye Shantao, a director of the bank, accusing him of forging a letter from the deceased Huang Chuqiu, which allegedly approved Ye's resignation as a director, in an attempt to evade debt liability. The initial trial found the plaintiff's reasoning insufficient and acquitted Ye. Dong and others were dissatisfied and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court through Yan Luqing. The court had previously summoned [those involved], as reported in previous newspapers. The continuation of the trial was scheduled for the day before yesterday, but the key witness, Gan Yuesong, failed to appear. According to the appellant, Ye Shantao, Gan Yuesong initially agreed to appear as a witness but, unexpectedly, on the day before the trial, he suddenly claimed he was British and unwilling to appear in court without a British consular summons. Therefore, he was absent. Subsequently, Judge Zhao handed over the Riyue Bank's account books to Ye for review and questioned him about entries indicating he was a director and received carriage allowance [夫馬費]. Ye claimed he only served as a consultant for the bank and received carriage allowance as a consultant. The court stated that the key to the case lay in the authenticity of the letter. Since Gan Yuesong possessed a letter from Huang Chuqiu, it was necessary for Gan Yuesong to appear in court to testify whether the handwriting of Huang's letter presented by Ye Shantao was the same as the one held by Gan, and whether both letters were indeed signed by Huang. Therefore, the court adjourned the case and rescheduled it to summon Gan Yuesong for further questioning.

Robbery on Suzhou Creek 97

One Suspect Arrested

Yesterday at approximately 11:00 AM, Madam Zhu Zhang, a local woman residing at 15 Gubal Road in the French Concession, was traveling on a small boat along Suzhou Creek towards Xiang. Passenger on Hexing Ship Dies of Sudden Illness 98

Letters Found on Body

Seemingly Returning Home for a Wedding

The Hexing steamship of the Zhaoxing Company arrived at the Longmao Warehouse pier in Lujiazui, Pudong, at approximately 7:00 AM yesterday. A passenger suddenly became acutely ill, unable to speak. The ship's accountant, Liu Shuming, ordered a tea server to transport him to the Pudong Hospital for treatment. However, upon reaching the hospital entrance, the man's face turned pale, froth appeared in his mouth, and he died. Liu immediately reported the incident to the Third District Public Security Bureau, which notified the local bailiff, Xie Along, who in turn reported it to the local court. At 2:00 PM, Prosecutor Shen was commissioned to cross the river to Pudong for an inspection. The deceased was approximately 20 years old, wearing a dark blue cotton-padded jacket and trousers. It was determined that he had died of illness, and no relatives were found. An order was issued for photographs to be taken and the body to be collected, pending identification by relatives. A letter and a diary were found in the deceased's pocket, along with a five-cent exchange certificate from the Dongsan Province Bank. The letter was addressed to Chen Runxi, care of Dong Fahe at Shihhezhi on the Middle East Railway in Jilin, with the address listed as Chen, Guangji County, Hubei Province. The tone of the letter suggested it was from a father to his son, stating that the son had been away for several years and the letter writer had just learned of the son's address. The father stated that the son must return home this winter, regardless of whether he had money, to get married. The letter noted that there had been severe flooding at home this year but the family was safe, so the son need not worry. Based on this, the deceased was undoubtedly Chen Runxi himself. The letter is now kept on file at the Third District for future reference.

Farmers in Jiangwan Trigger Landmine 99

Residual Poison from the Japanese Army's War

Liu Xiang Sheng and Shen Hualin Injured

Yesterday morning at approximately 10:00 AM, farmers Liu Xiang Sheng and Shen Hualin from Shenjia Zhai in Jiangwan were tilling the fields, preparing to plant flowers (referring to cotton). Unexpectedly, they accidentally triggered a landmine buried by the Japanese army. The explosion was loud. It was heard in quiet areas of the city such as Zhabei, and was even mistaken for artillery fire from Wusong. Liu and Shen were thrown into the air by the explosion. After landing, they were buried in the soil. After hearing the explosion, Japanese soldiers rushed to the scene and carried Liu and Shen to a Japanese military hospital for treatment. However, Liu Xiang Sheng and Shen Hualin were severely injured. Yesterday morning, the Japanese soldiers ordered villagers to carry Liu and Shen to the Jiangwan Refugee Association on Gulou Road in the Public Concession, using a wooden door. Liu's face, chest, back, hands, and feet were severely injured. Shrapnel had penetrated his skin, making him look like burnt wood. Shen was also seriously injured and over 50 years old. The association immediately sent them to the Chinese Red Cross Society's No. 33 Military Hospital. It is uncertain whether they will survive.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Discusses Solutions to the Silk Crisis 100

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry believes that the Chinese silk industry has reached a critical state. To find a solution, the bureau's trade guide has sought rescue plans from silk experts both domestically and abroad, and has prepared questions to solicit opinions from silk industry experts and silk manufacturers in various regions for compilation and discussion. The questions are as follows: (1) There are many reasons for the failure of the Chinese silk industry. In your opinion, what are the most important factors, and what should be improved first? (2) There are large quantities of silk and cocoons in storage in Shanghai and other regions. How should the government and the people handle them? Farmers will be unable to sell this year's new cocoons after they are harvested. What methods can be used to compensate them? (3) Since the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War in Shanghai, most of the old silk factories have been destroyed. What should be the future direction of silk production? (4) How will the American boycott of Japanese goods affect Japanese silk? Is it possible for Chinese silk to take advantage of this opportunity, and how should it be done?

Letters to the Editor 115

To the esteemed Editor,

With the utmost respect, I write to inform you that your esteemed newspaper reported a bombing in Hongkou and that the Korean revolutionary leader An Changhao, among others, was arrested at No. 27 Baokang Lane, Xiafei Road. No. 27 is my residence, where I have lived for many years, and I have never had any Koreans visit. An Changhao was apprehended at No. 54 in the same lane. I suspect this is a misreporting of hearsay. However, since your esteemed newspaper published this news, well-meaning individuals have come to inquire or investigate, which is truly distressing. I am writing to respectfully request a correction, for which I will be extremely grateful. With sincere wishes, Pu Baosheng respectfully writes.

Esteemed Editor,

In the news of the Huining Guild Hall's banquet published in your esteemed newspaper the day before yesterday, not a single word recorded as my speech was spoken by me. I hereby request a correction. Xu Bailong.

Dear Sir,

According to a letter from the entrusting party, Dada Steamboat Co., Ltd., the Shenbao newspaper on the 4th of this month published a piece entitled "The Resolution of the Dade Steamboat Disaster" which differs from the facts, and requested the investigative team to write to request a correction. Our firm's investigation of the aftermath of the Dada Steamboat disaster found that there was no compensation or compensation for the victims' families, as the matter was based on the resolution of the shipping industry council and the principles of civil and commercial law. Only the China Relief Society, upon the company's invitation, provided relief funds, which were used to send the families back to their hometowns. The actual amount of relief money was 2,400 yuan, which is far from the tens of thousands of dollars mentioned in your newspaper. As the lawyer involved in this case from beginning to end, I have all the records available for verification. I am writing this letter to request a correction to match the facts and maintain a friendly relationship. Respectfully, Lawyer Zhang Shizhao, May 5th.

Reasons for the Student Strike at Xuzhou Middle School in Jiangsu Province 117

Higher Normal Students Demand Funds for Study Tours

The Department of Education Orders Temporary Suspension Due to Lack of Provincial Funds

Supervisor Yi Sent to Xuzhou to Handle Issue; Faculty and Staff Issue Declaration

Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou Middle School, reorganized from the former Provincial Tenth Middle School and Seventh Normal School, is now composed of two academies at the site of the two schools. Recently, its management has been relatively stable, and Principal Xue Zhongtai is also regarded as a sound educational administrator. A month ago, the higher normal students in the first academy demanded study tours as per regulations, as their graduation approached, but the Department of Education ordered a temporary suspension due to lack of provincial funds. The higher normal students consequently went on strike to express their demands. Principal Xue's dissuasion was ineffective. The school petitioned the provincial authorities, which ordered a strict prohibition and rectification of the school's atmosphere. If disobeyed, the leading students would be expelled. Principal Xue was unwilling to take such measures, so the higher normal students united with the entire student body and went on strike, issuing a declaration against Principal Xue. Thus, the student movement began on April 29th. The teachers also left the school due to the environment, temporarily staying at the Jiangbei Hotel. Principal Xue reported to the provincial authorities and personally went to the province to seek instructions. The Department of Education replied to Principal Xue's telegram stating: (1) "Received your telegram. The students' agitation of their classmates and expansion of the movement is intolerable. You must still follow the previous order and take strict measures. If the students do not obey, a major sacrifice will be unavoidable." The county of Tongshan has been instructed to assist in handling the matter. (2) "Received your telegram. Instructed the county magistrate of Tongshan County to assist in handling the matter. This case must be strictly investigated and dealt with to rectify the school's atmosphere." After Xue presented his case in person at the province, the Department of Education has dispatched Provincial Supervisor Yi Zuolin to Xuzhou to handle the matter. Yi arrived at the school on the 3rd. It is anticipated that the authorities will take severe measures in handling this student movement. Because the students' declaration was misleading to the public, the faculty and staff issued a declaration under their collective names to truthfully recount the events of the student movement.

Local News

Regulations for Municipal Council Subsidies to Chinese Private Schools in the Concession 118

The Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council has formulated regulations for subsidizing Chinese private primary and secondary schools within the concession. Schools wishing to apply for subsidies should first apply to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau if they are registered schools. Blank application forms can be obtained from the bureau. Schools that are not yet registered can apply directly to the School Affairs Supervisor Office within the Municipal Council and obtain blank application forms from that office to fill out. The regulations are listed below.

Regulations of the Shanghai Municipal Council for Subsidizing Chinese Private Primary and Secondary Schools

Article 1: General Provisions

1. For the purpose of promoting education, the Municipal Council allocates a certain amount of funds annually as subsidies for private schools. Chinese private schools within the Public Concession that are deemed satisfactory in terms of management, facilities, and academic performance by the Municipal Council, and that are in urgent need of economic assistance, may be subsidized by the Municipal Council.

2. All schools applying for subsidies must comply with the provisions of these Regulations. Only those that are deemed satisfactory by the Municipal Council may receive subsidies.

Article 2: School Administration

3. All subsidized schools shall have a board of directors to be responsible for the operation of the school and the planning of finances.

4. The board of directors must urge the principal or director to handle student admissions and attendance records, and to keep all school income and expenditure accounts, which must be submitted for inspection at regular intervals.

5. The board of directors must fill out the academic affairs report form prescribed by the Municipal Council at the end of each academic year and submit it to the Municipal Council before September 1. If the Municipal Council has any inquiries, they must be answered promptly.

6. The board of directors must report all holidays or school closures during the year to the Municipal Council in advance (this includes regular holidays, special holidays, and closures due to infectious diseases).

Article 3: School Buildings and Equipment

7. All subsidized schools must have school buildings that are convenient, sanitary, and suitable for teaching. They must have the following features: (1) fire prevention equipment, (2) adequate sanitary facilities, (3) sufficient light and ventilation, (4) clean buildings and clear drains, (5) proper repairs, (6) suitable allocation and arrangement and other equipment for teaching.

Article 4: Faculty and Staff

8. All subsidized schools must have a principal or director to preside over the school's daily affairs and supervise the work of the faculty and staff.

9. All subsidized schools must have adequate qualified teachers. The sufficiency of the number of teachers and the adequacy of their abilities shall be determined by the Municipal Council based on the school's buildings, number of students in attendance, school organization, course content, and teachers' qualifications and the courses they teach.

Article 5: Curriculum

10. All subsidized schools must have a curriculum that complies with the following: (1) The teaching must be based on the curriculum and its outline determined according to the nature and organization of the school, and must comply with the educational guidelines and laws and regulations of the Ministry of Education of the National Government of the Republic of China. (2) School courses should encourage patriotism and good citizenship education, and should not implement teachings that could damage international relations or cause racial hatred. (3) The weekly timetable for each grade and the weekly class schedule for each class must be posted publicly.

11. Kindergarten classes must have the nature and equivalent equipment of kindergartens in order to be recognized.

Article 6: Allocation of Subsidies

12. The amount of subsidies will depend on the academic performance, financial needs, and number of students in attendance of each school.

13. All subsidized schools must have been operating for more than one year. The granting of subsidies and their use shall be determined annually by the Municipal Council.

14. The Municipal Council's subsidies will be issued quarterly each year. The payment may be changed or suspended at any time for good reason.

Chinese Anti-Drug Association Holds Student Essay Competition 119

Registration Deadline: June 3rd

Submission Deadline: August 29th

The Education Section of the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association issued the following notice yesterday regarding the holding of the fourth National Student Anti-Drug Essay Competition: "At a time when the Japanese are invading and the nation is in crisis, and when the voices for the public sale of opium are rampant, authorities in various provinces are issuing chaotic orders and setting up bureaus to extort wealth, the central government is turning a blind eye as if tacitly agreeing. There is nothing more heartbreaking than this. This association fears the scourge of opium and is committed to anti-drug efforts. We hold student anti-drug essay competitions every year, and we plan to hold them as usual this year. Among the country's academics, there is no shortage of enthusiastic anti-drug advocates. We hope that you will actively participate and work together on research, which is also one aspect of saving the country."

(1) Registration: From now until June 3rd. (2) Groups: Divided into middle school and university groups. Both men and women can participate, with no limit on the number of participants. (3) Format: The writing style can be classical or vernacular. University group essays must be at least 4,000 characters long, and middle school group essays must be at least 3,000 characters long. Writing must be clear. References should be attached to the end of the essay, along with a photo and resume (native place, gender, age, school name, department, class). (4) Proof: The essay, photo, and resume must all be signed and stamped by the principal for verification. (5) Submission Deadline: August 29th. (6) Judging: The judges will be hired by this association and will award points according to the following criteria: (A) Accuracy of factual investigation: 40%. (B) Clarity of thought structure: 30%. (C) Conciseness and sharpness of writing: 30%. (7) Awards: The first and second place winners in both groups will each receive a gold medal, and the third place winners will each receive a silver medal. The first-place winner in the university group will also receive 40 yuan in national currency, and the first-place winner in the middle school group will also receive 30 yuan in national currency. (8) Topics: Participants can choose one of the following topics, or they can participate with their own particularly novel and valuable topics: (A) The Japanese Imperialists' Opium Policy. (B) Efforts That Should Be Made to Ban Opium Amid National Crisis. (C) Public Sale of Opium and National Economy and People's Livelihood. (D) Steps to Eliminate the Conspiracy to Commercialize Opium. (E) Similarities and Differences between the Opium Sales System and Scientific Methods of Opium Prohibition. (9) References: This association has published many Chinese and Western books on anti-drug efforts over the years, with abundant materials for reference. If participants wish to purchase them, this association can offer a discount. Books with a total value of 5 yuan will only cost 1 yuan, but only during the registration period.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Frontline Stretcher Team Ordered to Withdraw 120

After the 19th Route Army retreated to the second line of defense, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Frontline Stretcher Team (incorporated into the 78th Division) also retreated with the army. The team leader, Ye Chunnian, also gathered a second group of team members and rushed to the front, abandoning their families and sacrificing their occupations, in order to seek long-term resistance through cooperation between the military and civilians. They have been working on the front line for three months. Now, due to the signing of the armistice agreement, the headquarters of the 19th Route Army will also move back. The commander of the 78th Division, in view of the end of the war and the fact that the voluntary long-term service of the team members was not a long-term plan, ordered the team to be disbanded yesterday. A notice will be issued to all officers and soldiers in the next few days to bid them farewell and send them back to Shanghai from Suzhou. It is reported that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce intends to issue orders to the companies and shops where the members worked before their departure, to restore their original positions as before.

President Zheng Hongnian of Jinan University Goes to Suzhou 121

To Inspect the Middle School Department of the University

The Zhenru campus of National Jinan University has been in a war zone since the Shanghai War broke out. Except for the university department, which moved to Shanghai to start classes, the middle school department was established in Suzhou, borrowing a part of the former Industrial College campus in Sanyuanfang, which has also started classes. President Zheng of the university went to Guangzhou some days ago to establish a branch school there. After completing the matter, he returned to Shanghai several days ago. Now that all school affairs in Shanghai have been properly handled, he took the Wusong steamer last night to Zhenjiang, and then went to Suzhou to inspect the middle school department of the university, and will return to Shanghai in a few days.

Silkworm and Tea in Huzhou and Xun Begin to Change 132

Heavy Rain and Stifling Heat... Silkworm Disease Spreads

Huzhou and Nanxun have always been famous silk areas. The silk from 輯里is sold well in Europe and America. Eighty to ninety percent of farmers are engaged in sericulture. In recent years, sericulture has been unsuccessful. This year, the silk and tea industries have both failed, and the rural economy has declined. There is nowhere to borrow silkworm capital, and very few people are raising silkworms, and the feeding amount is only about thirty to forty percent. However, they are all hatching foreign breeds, and the development after the receipt of the ants is still good. However, during the second eye, there were continuous cloudy and rainy days, and the cold and warm temperatures were abnormal, and silkworm diseases were everywhere. In the past two days, due to thunderstorms and stifling heat, silkworm diseases have spread everywhere, and there are many who have abandoned their silkworms. The silkworm harvest this year is also disappointing, and the silkworm farmers are very discouraged, it is said.

Qimen Tea Firms Feel a Lack of Cash 134

Robbers Are Rampant Along The Way

It Is Not Easy to Transport Cash

Qimen black tea has started to be picked and made for nearly a week. Recently, because of the good weather, the late tea in Zhou Shan has also revealed silver spears. The tea farmers in various mountains have successively opened the gardens, because the solar term has arrived. In the past two days, due to light rain and more sunny days, the tea body has been soaked in rain and dew, and the quality and taste have become thicker. It is very conducive to drying the embryos in the sun, and the shipments are quite good. The tea firms in the villages of Qimen Southwest and Fuliang have successively sent staff to weigh the tea and set up branches to search for and buy tea. Although the mountain price is slightly higher than before, the merchants are competing to advance because the tea stored in Shanghai this year has been sold out and there is no stagnation. They are rushing to box and transport the tea to Shanghai, hoping to get a new price. However, the weather is still cold, and the tea buds are not growing long. The tea farmers regret that the buds are too tender and are afraid that the harvest will be deficient, so they are mostly reluctant to pick and make as much as possible, and take their time to pick. Therefore, although new tea is on the market, shipments are not very active. Furthermore, the most difficult thing for the merchants at present is that it is not easy to transport cash. The reason is that there are more than a hundred miles between Jingde and Tunxi and Qifu. Robbers are rampant along the way. Although Jingzhen's cash is said to be sufficient and the foreign cents have been reduced, the merchants are afraid of transporting cash from afar in order to protect their capital. Even if there is picking and transportation, it will be difficult to manage in every possible way, which is very difficult. Therefore, up to now, all the cash of the various tea firms is not enough to handle the second batch of tea. It is not known whether the tea price, which is extremely high, will fall immediately due to the lack of cash.

Tunchi Tea Firms Suddenly Increase 135

More than eighty firms in the entire city

Have been leased entirely without exception

The tea market in Tunchi has always been known for its prosperity. In recent years, the selling price of various teas has often been higher than that of Wu (婺). At the beginning of this year, due to the impact of the Shanghai Incident, the money supply was severely restricted, and very few tea firms prepared to open. After the Shanghai market reopened, financial institutions were able to provide some flexibility and assistance to tea merchants, and the market situation improved rapidly. In addition, Tunchi's money houses, recognizing that local tea firms were generally stable and cautious in their operations, also provided substantial loans to maintain their operations. As a result, almost all firms in Xiutun have been actively planning to open in the past month. More than eighty firms in the entire city have been leased without exception. Furthermore, there are still more than ten new firms in the process of being established. However, before this ten-day period, bank drafts (申票) could be sold for 1,400 yuan per thousand taels of silver. Recently, due to the robbery at the Bank of China, all firms are guarding their cash reserves with caution, and the exchange rate has also risen compared to the previous ten-day period, with only 1,380 yuan being paid per thousand taels of silver. Tea merchants are indirectly affected considerably.

Grain and Rice Market Strengthens Slightly Due to Rain 136

South Shanghai: Yesterday, the rice market's inland sources included seven ships from Wuxi, Kunshan, Qingpu, Jiaoli, Fengjing, etc. Due to heavy rain in the morning, sales were suspended. By the afternoon, the weather had cleared, and six firms, including Hongsheng, Wanxing, Jiutai, Tongxing, Yishun, and Yuanchang, sold nearly a thousand piculs of early and late indica rice, with prices rising by one or two jiao compared to previous offers.

North Shanghai: Yesterday, continuous rain resulted in fewer people visiting the market in the morning, and the supply of goods gradually decreased. Furthermore, it was reported that the South Shanghai market suddenly increased prices, and trading interest was also weak. Due to the difficulty of transporting goods from the producing areas, thick indica rice rose by two jiao. The supply of thin indica rice was relatively scarce. A dozen or so firms along the river and rural merchants provided some support, leading to a price increase of about one jiao. Imported Du-brand pointed rice was selling steadily, and the market was stable.

Imported Rice Sales Are Strong 137

Jiangbei counties are requesting Shanghai to purchase imported rice

Yesterday, the imported rice market saw more active trading. In addition to merchants from Hankou actively buying, households from Chongming and Tongzhou in Jiangbei also made active purchases in the market. This was because the area had suffered from floods and famine last year, and their rice reserves had been almost exhausted. As a result, the local county governments issued a batch of permits, instructing rice merchants to purchase rice in Shanghai to provide relief. Currently, these permits have been approved by the Jianghai Customs and the Social Affairs Bureau for release. Only a portion of the permits still need to go through procedures before they can be transported. Once these merchants start buying, the market will see a significant improvement. However, two ships of imported rice arrived yesterday and today, and rice merchants were unwilling to raise prices sharply. Therefore, the selling prices remained largely unchanged from the previous day. Small-grain rice was offered at 7,000 bags, priced at 10.30 yuan to 10.0156 yuan. Keladi brown rice was offered at more than 2,000 bags, priced at 9.70 yuan to 9.60 yuan.

Oil Market: Production of Tung Oil in Hongjiang Is Severely Restricted 139

However, this year, the Shanghai Incident occurred, causing the market to be closed for two months, which prevented development. Since the market reopened, there has been no movement. However, the military situation in the interior has not been completely resolved, so it has not been able to return to its original state. Generally speaking, it will only prosper and become smooth after the money supply is circulating. Now that the battles on both sides are about to end, the revival of commerce can be expected. Firms in this port are preparing to re-energize themselves and find ways to promote their business. However, it is reported that the oil presses in the producing areas have greatly reduced production in light of the military situation in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. According to their total production, it is less than half of what it was in previous years. If this is true, then a reduction in supply is inevitable. Fortunately, sales are also not as strong as in previous years, which can be said with certainty. Even if spring sales are combined with summer sales, it is expected that there will not be a severe shortage. Currently, the selling price of the genuine Jichanghe brand is 23 taels, Jiyingfeng is 21 taels and 67 qian, the sub-brand Qingyuanfeng is 18 taels and 2 qian, Yanghengyuan is 18 taels and 4 qian, Xiangtaifeng Jifengying is 17 taels and 8 qian, and Liutongqing is 17 taels and 6 qian.

Gleanings of Humiliation Suffered by Compatriots 144

— Sun Choucheng

Yesterday I met a gentleman who had gone to Zhabei to move household goods.

He recounted the humiliation suffered by our compatriots along the way. It was infuriating. Alas, our country has not yet fallen, but we are already suffering the pain of being slaves of a fallen nation. If we continue to delay and the country falls, the suffering will be even more unbearable. Therefore, I have recorded the following from what this gentleman said, to express my sorrow and to hope that our compatriots will not go to Zhabei again before it is recovered, so as to avoid suffering. (1) About a hundred paces north of Han Bridge, there was a young man of about thirty, wearing a silk robe and woolen jacket, looking very neat. Unexpectedly, the enemy ordered him to hold a lump of coal, weighing about dozens of pounds, in both hands and stand upright on the side of the road. He was not allowed to move, so that sweat poured down his forehead. (2) On Zhongxing Road, I saw a man prostrate on the ground. Three or four enemy soldiers stood around him. First, they ordered him to raise his head and bark like a dog. Then they forced him to crawl on the street. One soldier chased after him. If he moved slowly, they would hit him with the butt of a gun, then throw leftover food on the side of the road and force him to crawl over and eat it. (3) A man was made to hold a burning piece of wood in each hand. He had to stretch his left hand straight forward and raise his right hand high. His face was smeared with black coal and mud. Standing in a rubble field, he looked like the Black Impermanence ghost enshrined in the City God Temple from a distance. (4) Paper masks were cut out and placed on the heads of children about ten years old. They were ordered to act like monkeys, jumping around incessantly. They were also forced to climb telegraph poles. They climbed and fell again and again. The children were exhausted and hoarse, and the enemy soldiers all clapped and laughed. (5) A worker bought a bundle of pickled vegetables in the market, intending to cook them at home. When he passed a post, he was afraid of their power and tried to avoid them. They caught sight of him and dragged him back. He was forced to kneel for an hour, and then they made him put the bundle of pickled vegetables on his head, so that the vegetable juice dripped all over his body. He didn't know whether to laugh or cry. (6) A fat teenager was slapped in the face four or five times by soldiers to test how crisp the sound was. When he was slapped, he was not allowed to turn his head, and he had to look them straight in the eyes. Otherwise, they would kick and punch him.

Occasional News from Yingzhou (Japan) 145

— Kaixu

The recent French general election did not have any major political upheavals that would attract our attention. However, even small news snippets can be used as a lesson for us to learn from and be moved by. There is a city in France called Pyrénées, located in the mountains, with layered peaks and very inconvenient transportation. They have repeatedly petitioned the French Ministry of Transport to improve the mountain roads and install telephones to facilitate transportation. As a result, the authorities did not adopt their requests. In this general election, all the people of Pyrénées unanimously decided to refuse to participate in order to show their resistance, which aroused national sympathy. As a result, on the first vote on May 1, no one in Pyrénées went out to vote. The French Ministry of Transport had no choice but to send someone to mediate and allow all their requests. Therefore, the people of the city have agreed to unanimously participate in the second vote on May 8. I have learned many lessons from this. First, the city's public opinion was unified and its actions were uniform. No one dared to defy public opinion and undermine it. Thus, it can be seen that the people of France are not as weak as the people of our country, and can be freely controlled by the authorities. Second, the government authorities can create benefits for the people and do not arbitrarily act alone. They follow good advice and do not become angry and arrogant, or go against the tide. Comparing them to us, how does the French Ministry of Transport compare to our country's Ministry of Transport? If a small town with rugged mountain roads does not even have postal services, how can it be willing to spend national funds urgently needed for military supplies to create benefits for the people of a small town?

(Starting tomorrow) The tenth year will begin with changes to this newspaper. It will focus on politics, society, economics, education, literature, art, and fine arts. The content is exquisite and very valuable. It is said that the annual subscription will still be only one yuan. The publishing house is located at No. 311 Shandong Road.

Sword Grinding Records

Pockmarked Liu 146

— Gu Mingdao

During the Battle of Shanghai, the 19th Route Army bravely resisted the Japanese. Although they were threatened by enemy aircraft and artillery, and by the large number of naval, land, and air forces, they were able to fight bloody battles for more than a month and repeatedly defeat the strong enemy. It is appropriate that foreigners should be respectful and admiring of them. Among the brave soldiers, foreign countries particularly praised the machine gun master Chen and the gunner Lao Zhang. But Pockmarked Liu, who was in the Big Sword Team, was also one of them, though his name was not well-known. Pockmarked Liu was named because his face had many spots. He was good at wielding the big sword, and was incomparably strong. When he was killing the enemy in Zhabei, he and his comrades first engaged in hand-to-hand combat and rushed into Dixiwei Road. Wherever the blade flashed, blood rained down. Many Japanese marines died under his blade. Therefore, his bravery was well-known. After the battle, he rested and liked to smoke a light pipe and talk and laugh. He said that he had pledged himself to the country and was fighting for justice, vowing to kill the Japanese invaders. He did not want to return alive. Later, the Japanese came to charge with tanks. Pockmarked Liu hung several bombs on his body and took the lead in engaging the enemy. He died in battle, but he destroyed an enemy tank with a bomb. Therefore, the enemy could not take advantage of his might. Zhang, from Dachang, fled to Shanghai and spoke freely about the Battle of Shanghai. That is what he told me. Alas, such as Pockmarked Liu, though dead, are still glorious. His courage is even greater than the ancient Ben Yu.

Record of Twin Towers in Military Service (43) 147

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Six: Pitiable Dream Night Forced into an Alliance Under the Bed, Still Remembering the First Time on the Mountain When She Carried Out the Window Agreement

If fortune favors me, I can set sail directly. I will become a rich and powerful man. Then I will keep a beauty in a golden house. It may not be inappropriate to wrong such a famous courtesan who has once dabbled in the world as a concubine. Thinking so bitterly, I still concluded on the focal point of seeking a way out. I suddenly remembered that Liang Xiaoyun had just planned for me. She has other shortcuts to go through. I couldn't help but want to ask more. I reached out and shook her fragrant shoulder, saying, "Sorry, I still want to disturb you. Because I've been feeling confused these days, I'm eager to find a way out. I heard you say that you have a way to get to Military Governor Ye Zuozhang's place. How should we proceed? Why don't we study it?" But Liang Xiaoyun's mentality was different at this time. Although she had intended to be with An Yutian for a long time, she was cautiously hesitant and did not act lightly. Because she has deep thoughts, she saw clearly that An Yutian is a young man with high ambitions and pride. It was not her intention to hook up with him casually. If she wanted to completely subdue him, with the condition that his love be undivided and never betrayed, she was afraid that he would be like a wild horse and would never submit to restraint. Now that she had this good opportunity to take advantage of his predicament and make him willing to swim up to take the bait, it could be said that the heavens had arranged it cleverly. She had already steadily caught and fished him. How could she not be leisurely and at ease? She just smiled slightly and said, "What's the rush? Since I said there is a way, I will naturally have confidence. There is nothing to study more." After saying that, she turned over and reached out to the tea table by the bed. She took a cigarette, lit it, took two puffs, and then turned around and handed it to An Yutian. He waved his hand, indicating that he didn't want it. She didn't force him anymore, just looked up at the sky and smoked alone, spitting out a series of circular clouds one by one, humorously appreciating herself. An Yutian curled up beside her, but did not have her elegance and leisure. After being hit with a soft nail, it was inconvenient to ask any more questions. Helpless, he felt very depressed in his heart and couldn't help but sigh deeply. Liang Xiaoyun heard it, and casually threw the half-smoked cigarette into the spittoon under the bed. With a "hiss" sound, it went out. Then, with a "puff" of laughter, she turned her face and said, "Are you really eager to study it? Okay. At this moment, I also suddenly remembered an important question that I need to discuss with you. For example, if I go to Military Governor Ye's fifth wife to lobby for you, if people ask what relationship you and I have, what should I say?" An Yutian was stunned for a moment, and stammered, "You can do whatever you think is best."

Commentary

The Fallen Society 148

Rui

Yesterday I saw in the newspaper two things, these things, in an evil society, especially Shanghai, can often be seen, everywhere can be seen, what I am saying today, is just using one example.

(1) Because the waist of Yang Xingying's cheongsam was too wide, a quarrel broke out between mother and daughter, and in a fit of pique, she threw herself into the river, and was rescued by a boat attendant, and lost her virginity.

(2) In the case of the Qi Rengxi family dispute, Qi usually indulged in extravagance and spent money like water. The sisters competed with each other to show off, resulting in a tragic end, and the result was so, which is regrettable.

I ask (1) what does it matter if the waist of the cheongsam is a little too wide, to the point of throwing oneself into the river and committing suicide. (2) A family that squanders money like this cannot avoid a disastrous day, these sins are all created by society, I can say that these two people are two representatives of the current society, like this, there are countless.

Since the Xinhai Revolution, everywhere has followed the example of Europe and the United States, and in recent days, this trend has become even worse. Originally, since the opening of the five treaty ports, the gate has long been broken, and it is naturally impossible to maintain a closed-door policy, but in following the example of Europe and the United States, one should follow the good points of Europe and the United States, and not the bad points of Europe and the United States. Now the good points of Europe and the United States, some have never been learned, and the bad points of Europe and the United States, it can be said that everything can be done.

For example, the representative system, which has been practiced in Europe and the United States for many years, cannot be said to be absolutely free of drawbacks, but it is generally a good system with more advantages than disadvantages. When it comes to our country, it is subcontracting, bribery, appointment, coercion, and the occurrence of various bad phenomena. As for modern women, they like to dance, watch movies, fold their chests and sway their clothes, and look strange and grotesque, flaunting themselves in the streets. Men wear suits and leather shoes, talk about freedom, talk about love, talk about Europeanization, and dress up beautifully, these are their life goals.

Therefore, the life of young children is very high, and the ability to produce has no foundation, they look forward to the occasional opportunity every day, and the arrival of good luck, one day they are successful, they can live in a western-style house, take a car, boast about their wives and concubines, and various delusions linger in their minds and cannot go away, and if they are unsuccessful, they are frustrated and bored, depressed and unsuccessful, the so-called "a fool looking up at the sky falling, a poor man looking forward to the people rebelling", and looking back at the old-fashioned family, like a beast trapped in a cage, and a prison prisoner a thug, so the right path is not followed, and many people run on the wrong path.

A good government must first have a good society, and a good society must have a good government to promote it. Now the national treasury is like washing, and the extravagance and licentiousness of the wind is rampant, the national productivity is almost equal to zero, and the westernization is imitated without the slightest detail, the country is in great trouble, and the social phenomenon is like this, what else can be said? What else can be said?

Science

Vitamins 152

Ji

The term "vitamins" can often be found in modern books, but what exactly are they? I'm afraid many people are still a bit confused. Vitamins are mysterious, invisible, and odorless substances contained in food. They are indispensable in our daily lives, because without them, we will be weak, sick, and even die.

According to scientists, there are now seven types of vitamins, but in terms of actual use, there are only six. They each have their own special functions and cannot be substituted for one another. Therefore, it is not appropriate to eat only one type of food, even if it provides a certain vitamin but lacks other vitamins.

Many inexplicable facts from the past have now broken through the mystery and found their causes due to the discovery of vitamins. For example, navigators and sailors often suffered from "scurvy." In the past, no one knew the source of the disease, but now it is known that it is caused by a lack of vitamin C. This vitamin is contained in fresh fruits and vegetables. It is difficult to obtain fresh fruits and vegetables at sea, so a lack of vitamin C leads to "scurvy."

Now, their functions and sources will be explained in order below:

Vitamin A: Its functions: (1) Prevents colds and microbial infections. It is found in milk, butter, fresh cream cheese, and eggs. (2) Maintains health and promotes the growth of children. It is found in green vegetables such as spinach and green carrots. (3) Prevents eye diseases. It is found in yellow vegetables.

Vitamin B: Its functions: (1) Maintains nerve health and prevents nerve diseases. It is found in wheat and other grain sprouts. (2) Increases appetite. It is found in animal liver and lettuce. (3) Helps infants grow. It is found in raw peanuts.

Vitamin C: Its functions: Maintains the health of blood cells and prevents scurvy. It is found in oranges, lemons, grapes, raw cabbage, pickles, sprouted beans, tomatoes, lettuce, peanuts, and spinach.

Vitamin D: Its functions: (1) Helps bone growth and prevents rickets in children. It is found in liver, cod liver oil, and egg yolk. (2) Prevents tooth decay and helps blood clot. It is found in sunlight and sunlamps.

Vitamin E: Its functions: Helps the growth of infants in the mother's body. It is found in wheat and grain germ oil and vegetable oil.

Vitamin F: Its functions are the same as Vitamin B.

Vitamin G: Its functions: Prevents skin diseases. It is found in fresh milk, liver, green vegetables, bananas, and fermented products.

Now that we know their functions and sources, and at the same time realize what kind of vitamins we lack, then it will not be difficult to arrange our daily food configuration.

Suddenly, a group of female students came, and he opened his mouth to say, "Miss…". You old fool! It scared me! The beggar sneered and said, "If I were a minister, a director, a doctor, or a master, you might not dislike me for being old, and you would sing praises in front of me."

After hearing this, I came back and thought about it. Why are the sacred female students only focused on vanity and power! This old beggar was really hit by this."

Correction

Defending Lu Zengxiang 155

— Wang Zhaoxiang

In Mr. Bai Tao's article ("Who is the Traitor"), it says ("Who exactly is the traitor who signed the treaty of national betrayal? It is none other than Lu Zengxiang, one of the notorious trio of national traitors, Cao, Lu, and Zhang.")

Mr. Bai Tao has misremembered. The Lu in the notorious trio of national traitors, Cao, Lu, and Zhang, is Lu Zongyu, courtesy name Runsheng, from Haining, Zhejiang, not Lu Zengxiang. Everyone knows this. As for whether Lu Zengxiang was a co-signer of the Twenty-One Demands, I do not know, so I dare not make a definitive statement, because the Northern Government did not clearly announce it at the time. Wang Jingwei mistakenly identified Xiong Xiling as a co-signer, probably for the same reason?

It is also said ("Lu Zengxiang, because he signed the treaty of national betrayal, regretted it too late, and now abandoned his family and became a monk abroad.") As far as I know, Lu Zengxiang's motive for becoming a monk abroad was to fulfill the dying wish of his foreign wife "a Belgian woman", and probably not because he regretted it too late? The dying wish of his Belgian wife was published in Shanghai newspapers before. (To be continued)

Bulletin Board

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 157

Criminal Judgments: The Police Department v. Hu Binggui, Opium Case (Main Text): Hu Binggui is fined ninety yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If he is unable to pay the fine, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, two opium lamps, two opium needles, and two opium trays are all confiscated and burned. ▲ The Police Department v. Li Liu, Opium Case (Main Text): Li Liu is fined thirty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If she is unable to pay the fine, she will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, one opium tongs, and one opium tray are all confiscated and burned. ▲ The Police Department v. Zhou Xu, Opium Case (Main Text): Zhou Xu is fined sixty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If she is unable to pay the fine, she will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, and one opium needle are all confiscated and burned. ▲ The Police Department v. Chen Akang, Opium Case (Main Text): Chen Akang is fined thirty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If he is unable to pay the fine, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, three opium lamps, two opium needles, and two opium trays are all confiscated and burned. ▲ The Police Department v. Wang Chen, Opium Case (Main Text): Wang Chen is fined thirty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If she is unable to pay the fine, she will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, and one opium needle are all confiscated and burned. ▲ The Police Department v. Lu Yusheng, Opium Case (Main Text): Lu Yusheng is fined fifty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If he is unable to pay the fine, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, and one opium tray are all confiscated and burned. ▲ The Police Department v. Wang Xiaogao, Opium Case (Main Text): Wang Xiaogao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for selling opium substitutes. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, it will be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. One and a half taels of red pills, ten jiao of foreign currency, and forty-four copper coins are all confiscated. ▲ The Police Department v. Wu Kaigun, Robbery Case (Main Text): Wu Kaigun and Ge San (i.e., Gu San), for three counts each of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, are each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment; for one count each of attempted robbery in collusion with weapons, are each sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment. All shall serve eight years of imprisonment. Jia Tongfa, for two counts of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, and shall serve seven years and five months of imprisonment. Chen Jigan, for two counts of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, for one count of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, and for one count of illegally entering a residence at night and committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. All shall serve eight years and two months of imprisonment. Hu Yongcai (i.e., Wu Yongcai), for two counts of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, and for one count of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. All shall serve seven years and one month of imprisonment. Sun Jinbiao (i.e., Shen Jinbiao), a repeat offender, for five counts of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment each; for one count of attempted robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment; for one count of receiving stolen goods, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment. All shall serve ten years of imprisonment. Xu Laosi, for three counts of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment each, for two counts of committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment each, and for one count of illegally entering a residence at night and committing robbery in collusion with weapons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. All shall serve nine years of imprisonment. Chen Yang, for possessing military handguns and ammunition without permission, is sentenced to thirty days of detention. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment and detention at a rate of two days for one day. Four handguns and thirty bullets are all confiscated. Gu Asan, Li Xiaoer, Wang Jinbiao, Zhang Erbao, Sun Lin, Fang Zhongshu, Jin Zhang, and Wang Yilong are all found not guilty. ▲ The Police Department v. A Quan, Opium Case (Main Text): Zhou A Quan is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined fifty yuan for providing his premises for others to use opium for profit as a repeat offender. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, it will be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Opium paraphernalia, red pills, etc., are confiscated according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Zhu Genfu, Opium Case (Main Text): Zhu Genfu is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan for assisting in providing his premises for others to use opium substitutes for profit. Zhan Youquan, Li Zhang, Wang Sanbao, and Yao Youxiang are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for using opium substitutes. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, it will be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Li Zhang and Yao Youxiang are given a two-year suspended sentence. Opium pipes, red pills, etc., are confiscated according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Wang Li, Opium Case (Main Text): Wang Li is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for providing her premises for others to use opium and opium substitutes for profit. Wang Rongsheng and Li Lanting are sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for using opium substitutes. Xu Jiadou is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for using opium. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, it will be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Li Lanting and Xu Jiadou are given a two-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia, red pills, silver dollars, copper coins, etc., are confiscated according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Yin Ade, Opium Case (Main Text): Yin Ade is sentenced to eight months of imprisonment and fined two hundred yuan for providing his premises for others to use opium substitutes for profit. Liu Agen is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined forty yuan for assisting in providing his premises for others to use opium substitutes for profit. Wang Meisheng, Qian Jiaosheng, Guo Hongsheng, Xie Ronglin, and Xu Renliang are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, it will be calculated at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Wang Meisheng, Xie Ronglin, and Xu Renliang are given a two-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia, red pills, etc., are confiscated according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Chen Hu, Opium Case (Main Text): Chen Hu is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing her premises for others to use opium substitutes. Xu Acai and Zhu Maoqing are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Four opium pipes and red pills, etc., are confiscated and burned according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Xu Heshang, Opium Case (Main Text): Xu Heshang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to use opium substitutes. Ji Wu, Gu Shougen, and Wang Ajin are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Five opium pipes and sixteen red pills are confiscated and burned according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Luo Laohong, Opium Case (Main Text): Luo Laohong is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to use opium. Liang Xihua, Chen Jiafa, and Fei Asi are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Chen Jiafa and Fei Asi are each given a two-year suspended sentence. Opium pipes, etc., are confiscated and burned according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Wang Adao, Opium Case (Main Text): Wang Adao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing his premises for others to use opium substitutes. Wang Qinglin and Zhang Shi are each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. Wang Abao and Wang Chen are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for attempted use of opium substitutes. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Two opium pipes and red pills, etc., are confiscated and burned according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Cai Wang, Opium Case (Main Text): Cai Wang is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for using opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Pu Genbao and Yao Xiutao are found not guilty. Opium pipes, etc., are confiscated and burned according to the list. ▲ The Police Department v. Pan Xiaofu, Case of Transporting Stolen Goods (Main Text): Pan Xiaofu is sentenced to twenty days of detention for transporting stolen goods. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the detention at a rate of two days for one day. Thirty-eight packages of red pills are confiscated and burned.

Shanghai Local Court 158

Criminal Judgments: Peng Agou et al., Theft Case (Main Text): Peng Agou, Gong Xiaomazi, and Zhou Laoqi are all found not guilty. The proceedings against Gong Yang are suspended. ▲ Yi Zhicheng, Embezzlement Case (Main Text): Yi Zhicheng is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for knowingly collecting fees that should not have been collected. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Yin Sinan, Theft Case (Main Text): Yin Sinan is sentenced to five months of imprisonment for stealing the property of others with the intention of possessing it unlawfully. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Zhang Xigao, Opium Case (Main Text): Zhang Xigao is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined eighty yuan for possessing opium with the intention of selling it. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. One package of opium paste, weighing thirty-four taels, is confiscated and burned. ▲ Wang Sanbao et al., Theft Case (Main Text): Wang Sanbao and Zheng Fuquan are sentenced to six months of imprisonment for committing theft during a disaster. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Lin Xuezhong, Interference with Family Case (Main Text): Lin Xuezhong is found not guilty. ▲ Nantong Prosecutor's Appeal Case Regarding Ni Qian et al., Injury (Main Text): The original judgment regarding the guilt and punishment of Ni Qian and Ni Sheng, and the part regarding Ni Mao's case being dismissed, is reversed. Ni Qian, i.e., Yan Qian, and Ni Sheng are each fined thirty yuan for jointly injuring a person. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the fine at a rate of one day for one yuan. The part regarding Ni Mao's case is dismissed. ▲ Zhou Dahai, Robbery Case (Main Text): Zhou Dahai is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for using violence to overcome resistance and forcibly taking the property of others with the intention of unlawful possession. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Wang Liansheng, Theft Case (Main Text): Wang Liansheng is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for committing theft during a disaster. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. ▲ Wu Xiaowu et al., Fraud and Escape Case (Main Text): Wu Xiaowu is sentenced to five months of imprisonment for fraud. The number of days of detention will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Qiao Heshang is found not guilty. ▲ Zheng Renye v. Wang Jingtang, Fraud Case (Main Text): This private prosecution is dismissed. (Above, May 4th)
